 pulicekarmiyon ne peechha karne ke baad main driver ko giraftaar kar gaiyr-iradatan hatya kaa maamla darj kar liya he
 This is the sixth time the Bharatiya Janata Party government has been formed in Gujarat
 vijay roopaani ne mangalvaar ko duusari baar rajya ke mukhyamantri pad kii shapath lee
 The results on 18 December have raised alarm bells for the Bharatiya Janata Party
 chunki pichley 22 saal main ye pehali baar he jab bijepi kii siten 100 se neeche gai hai
 The BJP government was on the backfoot on several issues before the election
 ab sarkaar banane ke baad bhi ye mushkilen kam nahin hui hai
 Along with taking oath of Chief Minister, these challenges are waiting for Vijay Rupani
 1
 Popularizing BJP in villages: The most important challenge before Vijay Rupani and Nitin Patel is to strengthen the party's position in the rural areas of the state
 beete chunaavon main jis tarah party ne gramin ilaakon main apni pakad congress ke haath khoi he usase kendriya netritv sakate main hai
 At the same time, in the wake of the 2019 general elections, Rupani and Deputy Chief Minister Nitin Patel, who are once again becoming chief ministers, will have to bring rural areas under the Gujarat model of development
 party ne is chunaav main gujarat ke chaar bade shaharon main hi sarvaadhik siten jiti hai
 2
 patelon kii naaraazgi dur karnavidhansabha chunaav ke nateezon main party kaa mahaj 99 siton par simat jane kaa bada kaaran aarakshan ke mudde par patelon kii naaraazgi ko mana ja rahaa he
 Just as Hardik Patel and the Congress Party have campaigned to separate the Patel community from the BJP during campaigning, the party high command is heard alarm bells for 2019
 lihaaja, vijay roopaani ke saath nitin patel ko netritv ke sheersh par rakhkar party ne donon ko jimmedaari di he ki patel votbank main hue nuksaan kii bharpai kii jaae jisase 2019 main unhen patel samudaay kii naaraazgi kaa saamana na karnaa pade
 Also read: Gujarat were losing, Jaitley made these bets and Modi won 3
 2019 main bijepi kaa kila bachaanavidhansabha chunaavon congress ke khate main badi siton ne bijepi ko kila ganvaane kaa ahsaas kara diya he
 Whereas in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, BJP has won all the seats in the state and strengthened Narendra Modi as Prime Minister
 lekin vidhansabha chunaavon main congress ke achche pradarshan se ek baar phir chunauti 2019 main piem modi ko majboot karne ke liye rajya kii sabhi loksabhaa siton par jeet hasil karne kii he
 In 2014, the party swept all 26 seats, clearing the Congress sweep
 aise main 2019 main ek seat bhi kam hone par party kii saakh par batta lag saktaa he
 4
 pehle se taqatvar vipaksh se vidhansabha main nipatnagujarat main bijepi sarkaar ke beete chaar kaarykaal main teen ke dauraan narendra modi khud rajya kaa netritv kar rahe the
 During that time, the Congress continued to play a weak opposition in the state
 lekin vijay roopaani kii pichhali bijepi sarkaar ke baad party ko antiinkambency ke asar se satta ganvaane kaa gambhir khatra khadaa ho gaya tha
 But even after somehow being able to save the credibility of the party, the Congress party will be present as a strong opposition in the assembly in front of the new BJP government
 lihaaja, is sarkaar ne bijepi ko vidhansabha ke raste rajya ke liye nitiyaan nirdhaarit karne main congress ke mukhar virodh kaa saamana karnaa hoga
 This time BJP will get stronger opposition in the assembly than before
